Saṅ Hyaṅ Hayu, ms. MalPol 161

Author of digital edition: Aditia Gunawan

Filename: DHARMA_DiplEdSangHyangHayuBnFMalPol161.xml

Language: Old Javanese

Repository: Nusantara Philology (tfd-nusantara-philology)

Version: part commented since without access_token with github actions api calls are limited – still working on it

Witness

  • Paris, Bibliothèque nationale de France, Departement des manuscrits, MalPol. 161
    • Physical Description: The manuscript is written on the gebang leaves, measuring 47 x 4 cm, 78 folios, 4 lines of each folio.

      It was described by Cabaton (1912: 254) and more recently by Agung Kriswanto & Aditia Gunawan (2019: 21).

Edition

… maturu ri rahina, kaliṅanya ana kopama ika saṅ manon·, rahina juga sira sadakala, təkkeṅ turu, təka laṅkahan deniṅ rahina v-ṅi, təkke pati, lāvan teja niṅ aditya, vahyattahita (?) apan ahiṅan·, tan t-ke jro niṅ umah gambira 20b lāvan i jro guha, tatan maṅkana teja saṅ hyaṅ pramana, l-pas sira riṅ bava samaṅke, trus ikaṅ svagga patala, sapta svagga, sapta patala tovi, ava ata ya kasuluhan deniṅ teja saṅ hyaṅ pramana, kadi tatan pahiṅan ikaṅ lor kidul kulvan vetan isor i ruhur, maṅkana tatan pahiṅan teja saṅ hyaṅ pramana/

niṅ sabda, tan pāna katunan sabda maganalliṅ hiḍap ṅaranya pinaka panon pinaka paṅrəṅə̄, pinaka paṅambuṅ pinaka paṅasparsa (?) paṅrasa pinaka paṅhiḍap, li… hiḍap ṅaranya, tan pavak tan parupa tan pavaṇ (?) datan -- kagamal tan kasikəp, sukṣma niṅ hiḍap ṅaranya, tan kevəhan saparanya, trus iṅkaṅ gunuṅ denya, ndatan patapak tan pavuri, təpvit (?) luṅya t-kā meṅgal, adhyatmikaniṅ hiḍap ṅaranya, trus ikaṅ agəṅ aḍ-mit deni hiḍap, sapta patala sapta buvana isor i ruhur kapva kasuluhan katə/

nya riṅ sarira ataya lima, ndya lvirnya nihan·, srotendriya ṅaran ikaṅ hadas yan mijil riṅ taliṅa pinaka paṅrəṅə sabdha, gronendriya ṅaran yan vijil riṅ iruṅ pinaka paṅambuṅ ganda, jipvendriya ṅaran yan vijil ri lidah pinaka paṅrasa riṅ (sadasa/sadrasa) tvakindriya (?) ṅaran yan vijil ri kulit

-- pinaka paṅasparsa paṅhiḍap nastisa (?) cakṣu..randriya ṅaran yan vijil riṅ mata, pinaka panon ri rupa vanda (?), nāhan lvir ni kavijilan ikaṅ hiḍap lima rikeṅ sarira, mataṅnyan panaṅgah pañcendriya de saṅ seva sogata, ndan ikaṅ hiḍap an pa/

riṅ tutuk, tan v-naṅ taṅ bayu panulup saṅkakala, yan m-tu mahavan riṅ iruṅ, apan paṅambuṅ gandha pak..a nika, yan m-tu mahavan riṅ tutuk ikaṅ bayu an pakaṅaran habhab (?) v-naṅ ya panulup saṅkakala, apan maṅkana -- paknanika, ndan ikaṅ bayu m-tu mahavan riṅ tutuk mvaṅ riṅ ruṅta, tuṅgal ika kunaṅ apan najəjəg ya ri visayanya, apan dvaranya ya malenlenakanya, maṅkana tekaṅ hiḍap an paḍa tətəg ya ri visayanya, tan v-naṅ makavisaya visayani rovanya, apan ya dvaranya yan malenlenakə/

mva pva liṅ ni tatva, mati pveka saṅ paṇḍita, bayunira ikaṅ masuk m-tu ri ruṅnira, yata misan m-gil riṅ abyantara, yata sinaṅguh akasa paramata

22b ṅaranya ya sinaṅgah lina ṅaranya, umapa lvir iṅ lina ṅaranya, tan palviṅ, mapa rupanya tan parupa, apa lakṣaṇanya tan palaksana, apa hiḍap, ih umapeki ta karih iṅət-iṅət rasa niṅ aturu tan paṅipi, iniṅət-iṅət rasa niṅ aturu tan paṅipi kat-mu rasa niṅ kupa, pinih rasa niṅ si lupa kat-mu ta rasa niṅ nora hiniḍapnya, tan suka tan duhka, tan grahya tan grahaka,… saṅ hyaṅ ṅadma v-kasan lāvan saṅ hyaṅ ṅasiva. Animan ṅaranya alit, ahiman ṅaranya agəṅ, mahiman ṅaranya adoh, lagiman ṅaranya selpra (?),

25b prapti ṅaranya t-ka, prakampa ṅaranya magavay·, isitva ṅaranya basa, vasitva ṅaranya maṅāku, nāhan arta ni aṣṭaguna kavruhana saṅ sevaka darmma. Jñaṇa ṅaranya ambək tuṅgaṅ ah-niṅ ṅalilaṅ, vijñana ṅaranya, ambak branta magələh, kavijñan pan ṅaranya ambak t-ka yan akroddha, mamrap mamati, nāhan (ata/arta) niṅ jñana vijñana kavijñanan ṅaranya kaya/
